G1ConcurrentMarkThread::concurrent_cycle_start() {\n268:   _cm->concurrent_cycle_start();\n269: }\n270: \n271: void G1ConcurrentMarkThread::concurrent_mark_cycle_do() {\n272:   HandleMark hm(Thread::current());\n273:   ResourceMark rm;\n274: \n275:   // We have to ensure that we finish scanning the root regions\n276:   // before the next GC takes place. To ensure this we have to\n277:   // make sure that we do not join the STS until the root regions\n278:   // have been scanned. If we did then it's possible that a\n279:   // subsequent GC could block us from joining the STS and proceed\n280:   // without the root regions have been scanned which would be a\n281:   // correctness issue.\n282:   //\n283:   // So do not return before the scan root regions phase as a GC waits for a\n284:   // notification from it.\n285:   //\n286:   // For the same reason ConcurrentGCBreakpoints (in the phase methods) before\n287:   // here risk deadlock, because a young GC must wait for root region scanning.\n288:   //\n289:   // We can not easily abort before root region scan either because of the\n290:   // reasons mentioned in G1CollectedHeap::abort_concurrent_cycle().\n291: \n292:   // Phase 1: Scan root regions.\n293:   if (phase_scan_root_regions()) return;\n294: \n295:   // Phase 2: Actual mark loop.\n296:   if (phase_mark_loop()) return;\n297: \n298:   // Phase 3: Rebuild remembered sets and scrub dead objects.\n299:   if (phase_rebuild_and_scrub()) return;\n300: \n301: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/jdk--742e735d@b394eab7f7a9ef928dbbcac1e27e0a0b1577894a/-/blob/src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMarkThread.cpp%3FL200-300"}}}
